border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: square;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读，找不到合适素材的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">每日早读一句话之外，想要学习更多语音精讲内容的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">学过语音课程后，想进一步巩固、坚持影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: square;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读，找不到合适素材的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">每日早读一句话之外，想要学习更多语音精讲内容的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">学过语音课程后，想进一步巩固、坚持影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">有一定发音基础，想做影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想要提高英语发音、提高英语听力的你</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></li></ul></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: style="box-sizing: border-box;">是自主练习英语发音的秘诀！</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 14px;line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. be so/less judgmental about... 对...过多评判 </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">judge v. 断定；评价</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">judgment n. 意见，看法</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">judgmental adj. 动辄批评人的，爱品头论足的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You must try not to be so <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你该试着不对别人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">妄加批评</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You're being too <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">judgemental</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你太<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">武断</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I feel more alert, more positive, and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">less judgmental</span></em></strong> of other people.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得自己更警觉，更积极，对别人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">少些评判</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>They're not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">judgmental.</span></em></strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道你觉得我很<strong style="box-sizing: supermarket.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他在一家超市<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">公然</strong>行窃。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Now I have to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在我还得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">公开</strong>忏悔，不然就难以生存。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcDXibDpJdrpQrOT83mHI1qTY7Zac1JRUmKONhUicgzXpFibQwwWambBOF6o0xhYSnaKrqZx0pj8muqQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《黑吃黑》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">…or react <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">openly </span></em></strong>to what I'm about to tell you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">也别对我所说的表现出任何反应。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 2729.41px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 2729.41px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 2729.41px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 2729.41px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.612037" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcDXibDpJdrpQrOT83mHI1qT5ILMVfuYMAj3Zt21fcuicb0HpiafrBbxsV1Uicy4iaZCCEwjpbabcYcia2Q/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《24小时》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. So should we. 我们也是。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">*so+助动词+主语，表示“同样”、“也一样”的意思。这一结构用来对前面的内容进行回答或补充。须注意词序。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"I'm allergic to nuts." "<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">So is my brother</span></em></strong>."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“我对坚果过敏。<g style="box-sizing: border-box;">”“</g><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我弟弟也是</strong>。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Louise can dance beautifully, and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">so can her sister</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">路易丝舞跳得很好，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">她妹妹跳得也好</strong>。<span style="text-align: center;font-size: 16px;"></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, judgmental </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="line-height: 2;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: 0.701961);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">【老外说】是一档以“采访”老外为主的节目，帮助大家更好的了解中西文化差异，一窥英国人、美国人日常生活。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">每周一更新。本栏目适合精听/泛听。可做听写练习。</strong></p><section></section><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-bottom: -5px;width: 5px;height: 5px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></section><section style="border-left-width: 5px;border-left-style: solid;border-color: rgb(255, 222, 3);border-bottom-width: 5px;border-bottom-style: solid;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(214, 240, 252);text-align: left;padding: 10px 0px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">神游海底，看自由自在的鱼儿海龟，看五光十色的珊瑚海藻，相信许多人都心向往之。随着潜水运动风靡全球，走进水中世界已不再是一个童话般的心愿，而是一份令您惊喜不已的浪漫。今天采访到的这位老外曾经就是一名潜水教练，让我们一起来听听他的故事吧。</p></section></section><section style="margin-left: auto;margin-top: -5px;width: 5px;height: 5px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;padding: 15px 10px 25px;border-top-left-radius: 1em;border-top-right-radius: 1em;border-bottom-right-radius: 1em;border-bottom-left-radius: 1em;margin-bottom: -30px;background-color: rgb(254, 244, 234);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> No, I don't actually have any New Year's resolutions for next year, but there are things that I would like to do next year. I would like to go diving more often. I had a bad experience about a year ago, actually. And I didn't dive for about eight months. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDamMAgW9zmpe5nYgnLR2uEXYrkDDPMAeZYXiauurPjJQvRxPwKIAhWow/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/vvy0r1KqBMV1Qb1OxqWAbaNSFlHQeTJKUFZUoddSvziaROPFAMaFSXRO4BSB1BUhicw4k0icfG59hFC5AiafvBhwZQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-top-left-radius: 16px;border-top-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-left-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What's that experience about? Do you mind?</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I was actually doing a season in Cyprus Teaching, working as an instructor in Cyprus. And I rescued a diver, not one of my divers. Somebody else I found in the water. Obviously a very experienced diver because he was on a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">re-breather (换气器)</strong>. He was wearing a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dry suit (潜水衣)</strong>, which was crazy, I thought, since it was so hot. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5277778" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDic3Ab5F5BDtam9MF92zYz3iaYkyvOMsq0WNtQ2OfZhO1C0l1iaVn0Ez1Q/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDiaoGaNoiaQVUgU4Dky55TfLotbLr6qT43n1icicwicbrnd03Rnf8RKoTUcQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="700" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">But anyway, he died. So I brought him up to the surface. I started to do what we call rescue seven. It was just a very disturbing experience. I got him back to the shore, did <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">CPR（心肺复苏，全写为 cardiopulmonary resuscitation，包括进行人工呼吸和体外心脏按摩）</strong>. In the meantime, I had somebody else called emergency medical services. But then after a while, I stopped giving him CPR because it had been well beyond 10 minutes. And I knew that  meant a maximum, but if it’s 10 minutes, the police obviously have to get involved in all the rest of it. And I had to give reports and then spend time with the police, go back out to the site several times and go through all the actions that I had taken.</em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.562963" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjD9cicpOj3T4r77kHyURiaIwB1ibzIcFFoQu4BVLGUQjhx0UI2qhqfVfIrA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">The<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> consensus (共识)</strong>, I think, at the end of the day was that he had serviced his re-breather by himself, which is a very dangerous thing to do, unless you know exactly what it is that you're doing. I think that he must have done something to his carbon filter.  I think the cause of death was officially a result of something to do with this carbon filter, which basically meant that he died without knowing which is, you know, I suppose is good news, but he would have just literally just faded away and not even known that there was any problems. He was just quietly died, I suppose.</em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">It was pretty <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">gruesome (恐怖的) </strong>because I could tell that he was dead before I got into the shore. I think the thing that sort of stayed with me was when I was walking back to my divers who are waiting by the truck, another diver came up to me and said, you're the guy that brought him out of the water. And I said, yeah, I am. And he said his wife and children are walking behind me. Would you like to have a word with them? And I was like, no, I know nothing about this diver. I think it's best that they talk to the people that he was diving with, because they'll have all his information. And I went back to my guys. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">As I was walking back to my guys, I heard the screams. There was his wife and his daughter and his son, who's probably about nine years of age, something of that, 9, 10, I think from what I could remember seeing. And the daughter was much older probably about 13. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">That really sort of stayed with me. And then I was actually back diving. That afternoon, same spot. And then after a while, I was just going through the motions, actually. I felt that there was somebody on my shoulder all the time. So I kept on looking around, kind of like a ghost or something on my shoulder. In the end, I just realized that I I'm not enjoying this any more. I'm just going through the motions. I thought I should take a break from diving for a while. But it lasted a lot longer. I honestly had no <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">compulsion (欲望、冲动)</strong>, and there's something that I truly enjoy doing. It took me a long time to get back into water again. So even though I'm an instructor, I have no desire to go diving as an instructor anymore. I just want to do it for fun because I find it relaxing. And if you're just leisurely diving, not doing anything crazy, like going down to doing a deep dive and diving <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">wrecks and caves (残骸和洞穴)</strong>--these are the things that I like to do. Then it is incredibly safe.</em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6685185" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjD6WicWibkgC03KibPiaXhpv4ThTSohO3lYXmSfhqAOB72EXvy8Sg70ZnLMQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6666667" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDv5z1AclqoQG91SHmI9ANZaPtbwS0ztEIl5Wf8zmicwJopPb35rpmqew/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="900" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I think that once you've been underwater and experience the whole scuba experience, it really grabs you because the sights, the things that you are able to see, and the fact that you can stay there with it for as long as you can, for as long as the fish, or whatever it may be, is there, it’s quite something, but it's also very, very peaceful. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDamMAgW9zmpe5nYgnLR2uEXYrkDDPMAeZYXiauurPjJQvRxPwKIAhWow/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/vvy0r1KqBMV1Qb1OxqWAbaNSFlHQeTJKUFZUoddSvziaROPFAMaFSXRO4BSB1BUhicw4k0icfG59hFC5AiafvBhwZQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="20" 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you feel the water pressure? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">No, actually, you don't. But the one thing that you will notice is that your air, the deeper that you go, your air does not last very long. So that's why deep dives are great. If you're going down to do something specific, like dive a wreck or something like that, but your dive time will be that much shorter because of it. </em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">In a shallow dive my air will last well over an hour. On a deep dive, my air will last maybe only 20 minutes. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDamMAgW9zmpe5nYgnLR2uEXYrkDDPMAeZYXiauurPjJQvRxPwKIAhWow/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/vvy0r1KqBMV1Qb1OxqWAbaNSFlHQeTJKUFZUoddSvziaROPFAMaFSXRO4BSB1BUhicw4k0icfG59hFC5AiafvBhwZQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-top-left-radius: 16px;border-top-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-left-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It reminds me of the other day, I saw a video. There are a bunch of people, they dive quite deep, but without any equipment. They don't have any oxygen equipment. They just hold their breath.</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Free divers, yeah, I don't know how they do it. Honestly, I don't know how they do it. They go down to deep depths and they hold their breath for a long time.</em></p><p style="text-align: center;"><img class="rich_pages js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.7067510548523207" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDicdSRGfGvfe0StHkHRF3d6hulicAGAJDXr3cz43jk3sW4LmwvYicfOxBw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style=""/></p><p style="text-align: center;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">But at the depth of these guys go to their lungs contract to the size of a small orange. And it is dangerous. I mean, to do what they do, it can be very, very dangerous. I can't do that. It’s hard work as well. And you need to train and train and train. I used to know another diver and this is what he had started to do. And it's not easy. And it takes a long time to build up your ability to dive certainly down to the depths that you're probably looking at on that video. That's something that would probably take years to do.</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">I like to be easy with life. powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: At the end…</em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 60px;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 40px;margin: 5px 10px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9986245" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKclzkia2dXb6edDkAEUPiaAjDamMAgW9zmpe5nYgnLR2uEXYrkDDPMAeZYXiauurPjJQvRxPwKIAhWow/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="727" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen</p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 75%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: top;margin-top: 29px;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.85" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/vvy0r1KqBMV1Qb1OxqWAbaNSFlHQeTJKUFZUoddSvziaROPFAMaFSXRO4BSB1BUhicw4k0icfG59hFC5AiafvBhwZQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="20" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;width: 85%;margin-top: 11px;border-top-left-radius: 16px;border-top-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-right-radius: 16px;border-bottom-left-radius: 16px;background-color: rgb(255, 228, 200);padding: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The young man chose to die in the deep blue sea. </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Yeah, I'm not quite sure how it happened. Actually, I suppose, it’s the same thing, but he might have been in <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">narcosis (麻醉状态)</strong>. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Nitrogen (氮气)</strong> narcosis is when you spend too long at depth, and there's an excess build up of nitrogen in your body. The effects of it actually can be very painful and obviously can lead to death. But the effects of it, there's a feeling of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">euphoria (极度兴奋)</strong>, Complete disregard for safety. You can become <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fuddled (思路不清的，头脑糊涂的) </strong>and not know which way is up and which way is down and all the rest of it. But you just have this amazing feeling of euphoria and complete disregard for safety and danger and stuff like that. I've talked to several other divers who've seen that movie and the consensus is accomplish or is that in the movie, the illusion is that is that he probably had nitrogen narcosis, because if you remember, he leaves the line and goes off to swim with the dolphin.  As a diver, I really sort of connected with that movie. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">authentic /ɔːˈθentɪk $ ɒː-/ adj.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">done or made in the traditional or original way真正的；真品的；真迹的；真实的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a combination of authentic Cantonese tastes and textures.·它融合了正宗的广东风味和口感。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">as sick as a dog 病得厉害；病入膏肓</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was as sick as a dog, so I was unable to sit the examination.我病得厉害，无法参加考试。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There's life in this old dog yet.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used to say that although someone or something is old, they are still able to do something</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">assess /əˈses/ v.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. to make a judgment about a person or situation after thinking carefully about it评估</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a report to assess the impact of advertising on children</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. to calculate the value or cost of somethingbe assessed at something 估算；估计</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> The value of the business was assessed at £1.25 million.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">early stage 早期的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> this very early stage in your career could be a good moment to start a business, for a couple of reasons.要想创业，职业发展初期是很好的时机。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">prostate cancer 前列腺癌</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">prostate n.前列腺</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">percentage /pəˈsentɪdʒ $ pər-/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> an amount expressed as if it is part of a total which is 100 n.百分比；百分率；利润的分成；提成</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The percentage of school leavers that go to university is about five per cent.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">presence /ˈprezəns/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">when someone or something is present in a particular place n.存在；出现；在场；出席</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Your presence is requested at the club meeting on Friday.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">urine /ˈjʊərɪn $ ˈjʊr-/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the yellow liquid waste that comes out of the body from the bladder n.尿；小便</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: i</span></span>tem<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>f vocabulary. I'm Dan…</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">大家好，欢迎收听英语六分钟。该节目向你呈现有趣的话题，纯正的听力练习和单词来帮助你提高语言技能。我是丹。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: And I'm Neil. We'll be discussing dogs being use<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>n cancer detection.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我是尼尔。在今天的节目中我们将讨论用于探测癌症的狗狗。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Everything ok, Neil?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">一切还顺利吗，尼尔？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I am so tired. O<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ne o</span></span>f my childre<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n is a</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">s</span></span> sic<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k as a</span></span> dog. I didn't slee<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">p</span></span> all night long lookin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">g a</span></span>fter them.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我太累了。我的一个孩子病得很重。我整晚都没睡一直在照顾他们。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: A<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">s</span></span> sic<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k as a</span></span> dog is a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n e</span></span>xpression meaning ver<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y i</span></span>ll. I'm sorry to hea<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r i</span></span>t. Tr<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y a</span></span>nd hol<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d on i</span></span>f you can.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">As sick as a dog </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是指病得很重。听到这个消息我很难过。尽可能的撑下去吧。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Don't worry. There's li<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">fe i</span></span>n this old dog yet.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">别担心。生活中总会遇到这样的问题。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Good. It's funny tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t y</span></span>ou mention dogs because the UK's National Health Service is currently assessing whether dogs can be used to detect early stage prostate cancer.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的。有趣的是，你提到了狗。因为英国国民医疗保健制度现在在测试狗狗能否用于探测早期的前列腺癌。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Amazing. Any success?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">太让人难以置信了。有成功的案例吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Let me ask you in this week's question. In what percenta<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ge o</span></span>f cases were dog<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>ble to detect the presen<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ce o</span></span>f cancer in urine? Is it a) 50%? b) 70%? c) 90%?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我先问问你今天的问题吧。在多少比例的案例中，狗狗能够探测出尿液中存在癌症？</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) 50%? b) 70%? c) 90%?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I'm going to guess a) 50%.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我猜是</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) 50%</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: We'll fin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d ou</span></span>t late<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r i</span></span>f you're righ<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span>r wrong. So, Neil, I say dog, wha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> do you think?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">稍后我们再看你的回答是否正确。尼尔，说说你对狗的印象吧？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In the darkness something was happening at last. A voice had begun to sing. It was very far away and Digory found it hard to decide from what direction it was coming. Sometimes it seemed to come from all directions at once. Sometimes he almost thought it was coming out of the earth beneath them. Its lower notes were deep enough to be the voice of the earth herself. There were no words. There was hardly even a tune. But it was, beyond comparison, the most beautiful noise he had ever heard. It was so beautiful he could hardly bear it. The horse seemed to like it too; he gave the sort of whinney a horse would give if, after years of being a cab-horse, it found itself back in the old field where it had played as a foal, and saw someone whom it remembered and loved coming across the field to bring it a lump of sugar.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">黑暗中终干有了动静。远方，一个声音开始歌唱。迪格雷分辨不清在哪个方向。有时，声音似乎从四面八方同时传过来，有时又好像就在他们的脚下。这声音低沉得犹如大地发出的声音。没有歌词，也没有旋律，却是迪格雷听到过的最美妙的声音。那声音如此动人，使他难以忍受。那匹马似乎也喜欢；它低低地嘶叫着，仿佛拉了多年的车以后．又回到了童年时代嬉戏的故乡，看见所记得和所爱的人拿着糖块，穿过田野向它走来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 汤姆，你在干什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 玩游戏。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 玩游戏？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不行么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你考试不及格，汤姆，你能告诉我是什么原因么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 对不起。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 对不起？为什么说对不起？你学习没有用功么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不是，只是这次的考试题太难了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What are you doing here, Tom?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Playing games.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Playing?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Why not?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You failed the exam, Tom. Could you tell me the reason?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm sorry.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Sorry? For what? You did not study hard?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No. The test was difficult, to say the least.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The scandal caused tempests in the newspaper.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那件______在报纸上引起阵阵风波。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">丑闻</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: oʊl/ </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. g</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>i</strong></span><strong>fts<strong style="color: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：have been doing XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">*现在完成进行时：have/has been doing XX；现在完成进行时用来回顾从过去开始到现在仍在进行的动作和情况，或表示到现在为止一直在做的事情等。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">have been thinking</span></strong></em> about you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一直在想</strong>着你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">haven't been studying</span></em></strong> very well recently.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我近来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">学</strong>得不太好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>Because you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">have been holding</span></em></strong> it since this morning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为你从今天早上就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一直拿着</strong>它。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>And we are all working and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">have been working</span></em></strong> for almost 100 years.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们都在工作，而且已经<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">工作</strong>了将近100年。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">These people <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">have been waiting</span></em></strong> for you. They <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">have been sitting</span></em></strong> here.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这些人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一直在等</strong>你，他们就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坐</strong>在那里。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: old 古老的书籍</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>词链儿：XX of old 往日的XX，从前的XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the knights <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. the legends and the myths</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>传说和神话</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：legend / myth</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>legend n. 传说，传奇(故事</strong><g style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>)；</strong></g><strong>传奇人物</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">legend</span></em></strong> of Robin Hood 罗宾汉的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">传奇故事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>myth n. 神话；神话故事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the heroes of <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">myth </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">and </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">legend </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">神话</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">传说</strong>中的英雄</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ancient Greek <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">myths</span></em></strong> 古希腊<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">神话</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcTia2BEAlsmUncrhoysiaOW1vYH5XNob79LaUbd7jqKXraPGgdwAbesb9H4liaa7n5pwW8Yw7ibNFKuQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. Achilles / Hercules / Spiderman / Batman</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ Achilles 阿喀琉斯</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">Achilles，也常译作阿基里斯、阿喀琉斯等，是古希腊神话和文学中的英雄人物，参与了特洛伊战争，被称为“希腊第一勇士”。</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">是凡人英雄珀琉斯和海洋女神忒提斯的爱子。忒提斯为了让儿子炼成“金钟罩”，在他刚出生时就将其倒提着浸进冥河。遗憾的是，阿喀琉斯被母亲捏住的脚后跟却不慎露在水外，在全身留下了唯一一处“死穴”。后来，阿喀琉斯被帕里斯一箭射中脚踝而死去。后人常以“Achilles' heel 阿喀琉斯之踵”譬喻这样一个道理：即使是再强大的英雄，也有致命的死穴或软肋。</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：Achilles' heel /əˌkɪliːz ˈhiːl/ 致命要害；薄弱环节</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think Frank’s vanity is his <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Achilles' heel</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我认为，虚荣心是弗兰克的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">致命弱点</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653512876&amp;idx=2&amp;sn=17df9ba539f5db6d8ad266fb4077fa36&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【“软柿子”英语怎么说？】">点击链接跳转回顾【“软柿子”英语怎么说？】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9064815" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcTia2BEAlsmUncrhoysiaOW1opPiceqhe2RiaUwPWQfWdHtk7PBD2wCDJicXyZNLPMfBviaQK0I0WctwAg/640?wx_fmt=png?x-oss-process=style/xm" data-type="png?x-oss-process=style/xm" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ Hercules 赫拉克勒斯 （古希腊神话中的大力神）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">赫拉克勒斯（Hercules，又译海格力斯），是古希腊神话中最伟大的英雄。神王宙斯与阿尔克墨涅之子，天生力大无穷。但由于其出身而被宙斯的妻子赫拉所憎恶，因此遭到赫拉的诅咒，导致其在疯狂中杀害了自己的孩子。为了赎罪，他完成了12项“不可能完成”的任务。途中还解救了被缚的普罗米修斯，隐藏身份参加了伊阿宋的英雄探险队，并协助伊阿宋取得金羊毛。</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">赫拉克勒斯英明一世，但却遭到妻子误会，在他的衣服上涂了毒，导致其痛苦难耐自焚而亡。死后升入奥林匹斯山，被宙斯封为大力神，参与了奥林匹斯诸神与癸干忒斯的战争，并取得胜利。最终和赫拉冰释前嫌，为了表示对他的认可，赫拉将自己的女儿青春女神赫柏许配给赫拉克勒斯为妻。</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">在今天的西方世界，赫拉克勒斯一词已经成为了大力士和壮汉的同义词。</span></em><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;"></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: (Spider-Man) n. 蜘蛛侠</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美国漫威漫画旗下超级英雄</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: the hang of XX 想明白XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get the hang of it</strong>?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听明白</strong>了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>3：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You'll<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> get the hang of it</strong> soon.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你很快就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">可以掌握</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">no offense (to XX)  无意冒犯XX</span></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>No offense</strong>, but you were kind of rude.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>我没有恶意</strong>，但你的态度真的很不好。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.562249" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/L4LJPfaSIKcDXibDpJdrpQrOT83mHI1qTOaV0ZHn578Z83DNBrWsglfRNzDHetibXZ9rCnpX6fHGdSIMArib8JO0A/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="498" style="vertical-align: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/w2ZUJgIFGG7jWuJjpDjpj1W1bibQZww4woZT6TksGfy7ahyDIAia2lHarPtaKTOgArOFpJS24T8HPrhJ2tn0uBvw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg");background-position: 50% 50%;background-repeat: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-width: 1px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgb(246, 255, 239);background-color: rgba(246, 255, 239, 0.79);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 20px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(45, 147, 86);padding: 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;">词链输出</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 10px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-start;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(78, 177, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我始终不知道怎么骑自行车。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 88%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">点击空白处查看答案</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 88%;height: 150px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: get the hang of riding a bike.</p></section></section></section></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;margin-top: -150px;height: 150px;"><section style="height: 100%;box-sizing: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(246, 255, 239);border-width: 1px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgb(172, 210, 135);padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKd5RDBYeVM5SZjKkdyYJpAxicRPhibOQrtQDga5CwBxpzYNKkSPUlnuicWmrvyhgOXITrOic7J4A7D5Og/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="258" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 1.8px;padding: 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">扫描二维码<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">关注我们<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding:
