0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">翻译|听写</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">编辑|排版 Claire</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;justify-content: flex-end;margin: -16px 0% -10px;opacity: 0.59;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style='display: inline-block;width: 80px;height: 26px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-image: url("https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/rxDTHnHhFWOh1ZRZZVmsLlJmVUyFHZkfaZs0yVRYceELnfEI5YlkDFEsDc7ET89OomVKAGX7sRaicpJLJft8mHQ/640?wx_fmt=png");background-position: 50% 50%;background-repeat: no-repeat;background-size: contain;background-attachment: scroll;box-sizing: border-box;'></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></sectio</section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.wet  /wet; NAmE wet/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.潮的；湿的；潮湿的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：covered with or containing liquid, especially water</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Try not to get your shoes wet. 尽量别弄湿了鞋子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.paw  /pɔː; NAmE pɔː/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（动物的）爪</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：the foot of an animal that has clawsor nails</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sometimes tiger paws and sometimes eagle claws.有时是虎爪，有时是鹰爪。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.certain  /ˈsɜːtn; NAmE ˈsɜːrtn/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.（不提及细节时用）某事，某人，某种</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：used to mention a particular thing, person or group without giving any more details about it or them</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Certain people might disagree with this. 某些人对这事可能不会赞同。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.fluffy  /ˈflʌfi; NAmE ˈflʌfi/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.绒毛般的；覆有绒毛的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：like fluff;covered in fluff</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a little fluffy kitten 毛茸茸的小猫</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.sophisticated  / səˈfɪstɪkeɪtɪd; NAmE səˈfɪstɪkeɪtɪd/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.（机器、体系等）复杂巧妙的；先进的；精密的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：(of a machine, system, etc.) clever and complicated in the way that it works or is presented</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">highly sophisticated computer systems 十分先进的计算机系统</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.bio-sensor  生物传感器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sensor  / ˈsensə(r); NAmE ˈsensər/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（探测光、热、压力等的）传感器，敏感元件，探测设备</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a device that can react to light, heat, pressure, etc. in order to make a machine, etc. do sth or show sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A sensor will tell that there's somebody there.感应器能探测到有人在那里。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bio- 生物的；人生的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">( in nouns, adjectives and adverbs 构成名词、形容词和副词 ) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：connected with living things or human life</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bio foods  生态食品</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bio medical  生物医学</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.sensitive  / ˈsensətɪv; NAmE ˈsensətɪv/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.灵敏的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：able to measure very small changes</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a sensitive instrument 灵敏的仪器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.parts per trillion (ppt)  万亿分之一</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">parts per ...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ppm (parts-per-million, 10)百万分之一</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ppb (parts-per-billion, 10)十亿分之一</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.board  / bɔːd; NAmE bɔːrd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.上船（或火车、飞机、公共汽车等）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to get on a ship, train, plane, bus, etc.  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Passengers are waiting to board. 乘客们正在候机。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">on board  在船上（或飞机上、火车上）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：on or in a ship, an aircraft or a train</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Have the passengers gone on board yet? 乘客们登机了吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.screen  / skriːn; NAmE skriːn/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.审查；筛选</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to check sth to see if it is suitable or if you want it</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I use my voicemail to screen my phone calls. 我用语音信箱筛选打来的电话。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">11.assist sb. in/with sth. 协助某人...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Two men are assisting the police with their enquiries (= are being questioned by the police). 有两个人正配合警方的询问。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">12.evolve  / iˈvɒlv; NAmE iˈvɑːlv/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.（动植物等）进化；演化</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：(of plants, animals, etc.) to develop over time, often many generations, into forms that are better adapted to survive changes in their environment</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The dolphin has evolved a highly developed jaw. 海豚已经进化形成高度发达的下颌。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">13.explosive  / ɪkˈspləʊsɪv; NAmE ɪkˈsploʊsɪv/ / ɪkˈspləʊzɪv; NAmE ɪkˈsploʊzɪv/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.炸药；爆炸物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a substance that is able or likely to cause an explosion</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">plastic explosives 塑性炸药</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Then two wonders happened at the same moment. One was that the voice was suddenly joined by other voices; more voices than you could possibly count. They were in harmony with it, but far higher up the scale: cold, tingling, silvery voices. The second wonder was that the blackness overhead, all at once, was blazing with stars. They didn't come out gently one by one, as they do on a summer evening. One moment there had been nothing but darkness; next moment a thousand, thousand points of light leaped out - single stars, constellations, and planets, brighter and bigger than any in our world. There were no clouds. The new stars and the new voices began at exactly the same time. If you had seen and heard it, as Digory did, you would have felt quite certain that it was the stars themselves which were singing, and that it was the First Voice, the deep one, which had made them appear and made them sing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">此刻，两个奇迹同时发生了。一个是，突然间，数不清的冷峻、战栗、银铃般的声音掺合到那个声音之中，与之和谐地组合在一起，但音量却高得多。第二个是，头上的黑暗中突然群早闪烁。不是夏夜中一颗接一颗悄悄出现的星星，而是在一团漆黑之中，霎时问跳跃出的成千上万颗恒星、星丛和行星，比我们世界里看到的要大得多、亮得多。没有一朵云。新的星星和新的声音同时出现。如果你像迪格雷一样亲眼看见和亲耳听见的话，你会相当肯定地觉得是腥星自己在唱歌，而唤出它们并使它们歌唱的是那低沉的第一个声音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你这些天在干什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我正在学下棋。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 学得怎样了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 教练说我比刚开始的时候下得好多了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What are you doing nowadays?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I am learning to play chess.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: How are you getting along with it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: The coach says that I have made a better fist of it than the beginning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He desires to ________ over others.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他很想支配别人。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dominate</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'>9.14 每日一句：</strong><strong><span lang="EN-US" style="text-align: justify;">Judge a book by its cover.  </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong><span lang="EN-US" style="text-align: justify;"></span><span style="text-align: justify;">以貌取人</span></strong></p><p border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">What we achieve inwardly will change outer reality.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. ach</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>ieve</strong></span><strong> /əˈtʃiːv/ 元音/i:/；辅音/v/，注意区分/w/；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. inwar</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>dl</strong></span><strong>y /ˈɪnwədli $ ˈɪnwərdli/中包含/dl/舌边爆破，也可以在/d/处发喉塞音；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>3. r</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>e‧a</strong></span><strong>l‧i‧ty /riˈæləti, riˈælɪti/包含四音节，一二音节衔接处有/j/音带出。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 把what we achieve inwardly 看做一个整体，做主语</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. inwardly adv. 在内心；秘密地</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <span style="text-decoration: underline;">managed to </span>smile, but <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">inwardly</span></strong></em> I was furious.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<span style="text-decoration: underline;">勉强</span>露出笑容，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">心里</strong>却很气愤。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>反义词：outwardly adv. 外表上，从表面上看</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Outwardly</span></em></strong>, the couple seemed perfectly happy.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">表面上看</strong>，这对夫妇似乎幸福美满。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And I've a notion that I'd take to bleeding <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">inwardly</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那我大概会随之<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">心中</strong>流血不止。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6222222" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfXDWibAwLfyLBWqee1nSiasTCPeBXqKPVsmBkicvgtYnIAD1AWTNBmP9xO1rysBgqUicTyPHJtVviaibFA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《简爱》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. outer adj. 在外的，外面的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>反义词：inner adj. 隐藏的；内心的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">outer</span> space 外太空</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">inner</span></em></strong> conflict is related to struggles in the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">outer</span></em></strong> world.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">内心的</strong>矛盾和<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外部</strong>世界的争斗有关。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>The <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">outer</span></em></strong> journey and the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">inner</span></em></strong> journey <span style="text-decoration: underline;">mirror each other</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外在的</strong>旅程和<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">内在的</strong>旅程<span style="text-decoration: underline;">互相映照</span>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>That's an <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">outer</span></em></strong> wall built <span style="text-decoration: underline;">all the way to</span> the edge of the reef.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那是一堵<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外</strong>墙，<span style="text-decoration: underline;">一直建到</span>珊瑚礁的边缘。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It better be bigger and more impressive than <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">outer </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">space</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最好要比<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">外</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太空</strong>的主题更宏大更震撼。</p></section><section 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px 1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: rgb(18, 17, 17);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">扫描二维码快速购买课程</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">或点击推送底部<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">“阅读原文”</span>购买</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px 1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px -1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1.4px 0px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1.4px 0px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 3.4px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 0.6px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: square;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读，找不到合适素材的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">每日早读一句话之外，想要学习更多语音精讲内容的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">学过语音课程后，想进一步巩固、坚持影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">有一定发音基础，想做影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想要提高英语发音、提高英语听力的你</p></li></ul></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.Burglary </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英/'bɜːglərɪ/ 美/'bɝɡləri/  近义词：[n.] felony</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 夜盗；夜盗行为</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">入户行窃;入户盗窃罪   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">burglary insurance [保险] 盗窃保险</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">commit burglary 犯夜窃罪</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">prevention of burglary [安全] 防盗</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'd got nicked for burglary.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我因入室行窃而被捕。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.Theft </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英/θeft/ 美/θɛft/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 盗窃；偷；[罕]赃物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">identity theft 身份盗窃，身份盗用</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">guard against theft 防盗</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">grand theft 重偷窃罪</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">auto theft 汽车偷窃</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has paid the penalty for her theft.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她犯的偷窃罪已受到惩罚。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.Trespass </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英/'trespəs/ 美/'trɛspəs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 侵入；打扰；冒犯；犯罪</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 过失；罪过；非法侵入；擅自进入</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">trespass on 侵犯；非法侵入；妨碍；打扰</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They began to organize a mass trespass.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们开始组织大规模的侵犯</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.Ex-burglars 有入室盗窃前科的人</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Burglars  英/'bɜːglə/ 美/'bɝɡlɚ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 夜贼，窃贼</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The safe was forced by the burglars.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">保险柜被窃贼强行打开。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.Deterrent </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英/dɪ'ter(ə)nt/ 美/dɪ'tɝənt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 制止物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. 制止地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">nuclear deterrent 核威慑力量</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Large fines act as a deterrent to motorists. 高额罚款是对开车的人的制约。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.Avalanches</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Avalanche 英/'ævəlɑːnʃ/ 美/'ævəlæntʃ/  时 态: avalanched, avalanching, avalanches   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 雪崩</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 雪崩;雪崩般塌落</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. (因大量涌至而)把...淹没,使无法应付</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Higher still the snow was ready to avalanche.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在更高处积雪随时都会崩塌。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.Earthquakes</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Earthquake 英/'ɜːθkweɪk/ 美/'ɝθ'kwek/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 地震</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">动乱, 大震荡</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The town was destroyed by the earthquake.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个小镇被地震毁了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.Biosensors</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Biosensor 英/'baɪə(ʊ)sensə(r)/ 美/'baɪo,sɛnsɚ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 生物传感器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The scientists say they are expanding their crayfish biosensor program into other areas where clean water course.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">科学家们说，他们正在把小龙虾生物传感器项目扩展到其他清洁水源的领域。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.Orthodoxies</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Orthodoxy 英/'ɔːθədɒksɪ/ 美/'ɔrθədɑksi/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. &lt;正&gt;正统观念;普遍接受的观点;正统的信仰〔做法〕</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">正教会;正教信仰与做法</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Orthodoxy is my doxy; heterodoxy is another man's doxy.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">缺乏怜悯的圣经正统信仰无疑是世间最丑透的东西。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Far away, and down near the horizon, the sky began to turn grey. A light wind, very fresh, began to stir. The sky, in that one place, grew slowly and steadily paler. You could see shapes of hills standing up dark against it. All the time the Voice went on singing.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在遥远的地平线附近，天空开始渐渐变成灰色。一阵清风吹拂过来。天上有片地方缓缓地、逐渐地越变越淡，映衬出群山黑色的轮廓。那声音一直在歌唱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我们布置了一篇关于世界水资源问题的作业，我一点想法都没有。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 为什么不到图书馆去看看呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 图书馆已经关门了，而我明天就得交作业。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 别着急，我这儿有几本与这个问题有关的书，也许对你有用。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I have an assignment on world water reservation. I have no idea of it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Why not go to the library?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: It has been closed now, but I have to hand it in tomorrow.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Don't worry. I have some books to the purpose. It may be helpful to you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A fine for ________ trash on public land; dumped the extra gear overboard.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因在公用土地上倾倒垃圾而受的罚款; 把多余的装备丢到船外。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dumping</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p 每日一句：</strong><strong><span lang="EN-US" style="text-align: justify;">to be honest </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="text-align: on ahead and do just what the hell you feel like. It takes a strong woman to stay by herself in a world where people will settle for anything, just to say they have something. </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. g<span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">o(w) o</span></strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>n a</strong></span><strong>head... 词间连贯；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. feel / will / hell 都包含舌侧音/l/。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">go on ahead 继续向前走</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Go on ahead</span></strong></em>. I'll catch up with you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">你先走</strong>，我随后赶上你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You hang around here in case he comes, and I'll <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go on ahead</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你在这附近等着以防万一他来了，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">继续往前走</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. what the hell </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">you</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> feel like  不管你想做什么</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">此处 hell表语气上的愤怒或强调</strong><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">试对比：</p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="width: 523.069px;font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">What was that noise?</p></li></ul><p style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">那是什么声音？</p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: disc;"><li><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">hell </span></em></strong>was that noise?</p></li></ul><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那到底是什么声音？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. <strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：</strong>feel like (doing) XX 想要做某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">用法：feel like doing something或feel like something</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He didn’t <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">feel like</span></em></strong> going to work.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想</strong>去上班。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">feel like</span></em></strong> another drink?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想</strong>再喝一杯吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, I really don't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">feel like</span></em></strong> hearing about my mother's past, especially from you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我一点儿也不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想</strong>听我妈妈的过去，特别是从你嘴里说出来。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1574074" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcmZicgWBTUqLm3h52z203ZLV0OqxMzhnT8qyRG7Hd7cl0ZNDQSiazrqTJT0WXNKhn9YVBbue4R88dQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《新飞跃比弗利》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. <strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：</strong>stay by oneself 独自生活，独处</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">stay by myself</span></em></strong> for a long time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可以一个人长时间地<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">独处</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. 词链儿：settle for XX 勉强接受；将就</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He wants a full refund and he won't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">settle for</span></em></strong> anything less.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他想全额退款，少一分也不行。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She never <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">settles for</span></em></strong> second best.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她从不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">甘心于</strong>退而求其次。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>And it's a miracle and it amazed me how little people <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">settle for</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这是一个奇迹，让我惊讶的是很少有人会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">满足</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>But we shouldn't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">settle for</span></em></strong> bad answers.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但我们不应该<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">满足于</strong>糟糕的答案。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, I'll <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">settle for</span></em></strong> his loved ones.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">知道吗？我会为他的挚爱们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">准备节目</strong>的。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style=" margin: 10px 0%; box-sizing: border-box; "><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px 1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: rgb(18, 17, 17);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">扫描二维码快速购买课程</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">或点击推送底部<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">“阅读原文”</span>购买</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style=" margin: 10px 0%; box-sizing: border-box; "><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px 1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px -1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1.4px 0px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1.4px 0px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 3.4px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 0.6px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style=" margin: 10px 0%; box-sizing: border-box; "><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: square;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读，找不到合适素材的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">每日早读一句话之外，想要学习更多语音精讲内容的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">学过语音课程后，想进一步巩固、坚持影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">有一定发音基础，想做影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想要提高英语发音、提高英语听力的你</p></li></ul></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Presence  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.  UK /ˈprez.əns/   US /ˈprez.əns/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">出席，在场；（事物的）存在，出现</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">仪态，风度；气质   举例：stage presence舞台风度</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Present   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK /ˈprez.ənt/   US /ˈprez.ənt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（尤指表示友谊或致谢的）礼物，赠品   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在，目前</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">出席的，在场的，存在的；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The whole family was present.全家人都在场</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在的，目前的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't have her present address.我不知道她现在的地址。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.  UK  /prɪˈzent/ US  /prɪˈzent/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">赠送，授予；提交；展现</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The documentary presented us with a balanced view of the issue.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这部纪录片向我们呈现了对这一问题的客观看法。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">主持播出（电视或广播节目）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She presents the late-night news.她主持午夜新闻。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">引见，介绍</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">May I present Professor Carter?请允许我介绍卡特教授。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a dog's life：a very unhappy and unpleasant life悲惨的生活</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">go through回顾；表达经历（困难，痛苦）；穿过某地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Catch </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">得病</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">赶上，  catch the bus</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抓住，逮捕；   I will catch you  我迟早抓到你</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bug  n.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（引起小毛病的）细菌；病毒</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There's a bug going around (= an illness that many people are getting).</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有种细菌引起的疾病现正在流行。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（计算机程序中出现的）缺陷，漏洞</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A bug caused the company's computer system to crash.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">程序缺陷导致公司的计算机系统崩溃。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">小虫子；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">窃听器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bug  v.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">烦扰；使…担心</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He's been bugging me all morning.他整个上午都在烦我。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">秘密安装窃听装置（这个常用于被动语态）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She suspected that her phone had been bugged.她怀疑自己的电话被人窃听了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Paw   n爪子，(informal)人类的手</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：Take your filthy paws off my nice clean towel!</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">把你的脏手从我干净的毛巾上拿开！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Paw    v. 用爪子抓（或扒）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When their dog heard them, it began pawing (at) the ground in excitement.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们的狗听见他们的声音就开始激动地用爪子刨地。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pad    </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（猫或狗的）肉趾，爪垫；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">垫，衬垫；护垫</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In the 1980s, shoulder pads were very fashionable in women's clothes.20世纪80年代，女性服装非常流行使用垫肩。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（直升机的）起降场地；（火箭的）发射台</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The hotel has its own helicopter pad.这家饭店有自己的直升机起降平台。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">睡莲的）浮叶</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a lily pad睡莲浮叶</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. （用软物）填塞，填衬</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">These boots are padded with shock-resistant foam.这些靴子加了防震泡沫垫。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Claw </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（兽类或鸟类的）爪，脚爪</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Our cat likes to sharpen her claws on the legs of the dining table.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们的猫喜欢在餐桌腿上磨爪子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（昆虫、海生动物的）螯，钳</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Keep your fingers away from the crab's claws when you pick it up.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抓螃蟹时，别用手指触碰它的钳子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Claw   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.（用爪子）抓，撕，挠</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was seriously injured when one of the lions clawed his back.他的后背被其中一只狮子严重抓伤了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So+助动词+主语:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">属于倒装句肯定形式,表示说话人的行为、动作和前面提到的人的行为、动作相同.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Neither+助动词+主语, 属于倒装句否定形式.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如:I didn't go to school. Neither did Mary. (Mary 和我一样,没有去学校.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">注意区分：So+主语+助动词:属于强调句型,表示说话人提到的事“的确如此”.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如: Tom likes English. So he does.(Tom的确喜欢英语)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hoof  n.（马、羊、鹿等动物的）蹄子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hoof  v. 踢（球）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The defender hoofed the ball up the field.防守队员把球踢向了前场。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sensor  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK  /ˈsen.sər/ US  /ˈsen.sɚ/   n.传感器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The security device has a heat sensor which detects the presence of people and animals.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">保安装置中有一个热传感器，能探测人和动物的存在。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Toxic  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.有毒的；引起中毒的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">toxic waste/chemicals/effluent有毒的废料／化学品／废水</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Methane  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.甲烷，沼气</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Methane is the main constituent of natural gas.甲烷是天然气的主要成分。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Used to do sth 过去常常做某事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Canary   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.金丝雀</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Cage   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.笼子    v.（把鸟或动物）关进笼子里</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">caged birds/animals笼中鸟／兽</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sam's been prowling about like a caged animal all morning.萨姆一上午都像困兽一样走来走去。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space:
