I aske<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d y</span></span>ou in wha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> percenta<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ge <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">f </em>cases were dogs able to detect the presence of cancer in urine? a) 50% b) 70% or c) 90%</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的，我问你在多少比例的案例中，狗狗能够探测出尿液中存在癌症？</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) 50% b) 70% c) 90%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: And I said 50%.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我选的是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">50%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: It's a dog's life, Neil. I'm sorry. The answer was c) 90%.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">很遗憾，尼尔，正确答案是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> c) 90%</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Wow! 90%! That's amazing.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">天啊！百分之九十！太厉害了！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Isn't it?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">谁说不是呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Shall we go through the vocabulary?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们现在一起回顾一下今天学到的单词吧？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: OK. The first expression we had was as sick a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> dog. If you are as sick a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> dog it means that you're very sic<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k in</span></span>dee<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span>. When was the last time you were as sick as a dog, Neil?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的。第一个表达是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">as sick as a dog</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，是指病得很厉害。你上一次病重是什么时候呢，尼尔？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Just after Christmas</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> I caugh<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span> bug<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> from </em>my kids. I was as sick a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> dog. Next we had paws. Paws are the feet of certain animals. They have pads and claws. Can you give u<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> few examples, Dan?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">就在圣诞节后，我受孩子传染生病了。病得很厉害。下一个单词是爪子。爪子是指一些动物的脚。他们有肉垫和爪子。丹，你可以举几个例子吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Well, dogs have paws. So do cats, rabbits, bears and mice. But no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> horses, sheep or pigs. They have hooves. After paws, we had biosensor. A biosensor i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> combination of the words biology and sensor. I<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t is a</span></span> sensor which use<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> living thing to detect chemicals. Can you thin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of </em>a</span></span> famous historical example, Neil?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">狗狗有爪子。还有猫、兔子、熊和老鼠。但马、羊和猪没有爪子。它们有蹄子。说完爪子，我们还提到了生物传感器。生物传感器是由生物和传感器这两个单词合成的。是指能够探测到化学物质的生物。你能想出一个历史上很有名的例子吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, Miners in danger o<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f a</span></span> highly toxic<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span></em> invisible gas called methane use<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to carry <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">a canary </span></span>i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span> cage down the mine wi<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">th</span></span> them.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">甲烷是一种看不见的气体，带有剧毒，矿工们通常会处于这种危险之中，所以他们会带着一只放在笼子里的金丝雀下矿。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There was soon light enough for them to see one another's faces. The Cabby and the two children had open mouths and shining eyes; they were drinking in the sound, and they looked as if it reminded them of something. Uncle Andrew's mouth was open too, but not open with joy. He looked more as if his chin had simply dropped away from the rest of his face. His shoulders were stopped and his knees shook. He was not liking the Voice. If he could have got away from it by creeping into a rat's hole, he would have done so. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">很快，天色已经亮得使他们能互相看见对方的脸了。马车夫和两个孩子张着嘴，目光闪烁，陶醉在美妙的声音之中；那声音仿佛使他们想起了什么。安德鲁舅舅也张着嘴，但不是出于高兴；他看上去更像是失去了下巴。他身子弓着，膝盖在发抖。他不喜欢那种声音。如果可以钻进老鼠洞来逃避的话，他会那么做的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你得到在剧中试演的角色了吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那个角色给了别人了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 怎么了？有人背后作了手脚了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 没有，我只是想说我得到了一个更好的角色。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 恭喜你了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 谢谢你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你看起来对这个新角色很满意。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是呀，它更有挑战性。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Did you get the part you tried out for in the play?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: The role was given out to someone else.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What happened? Someone did something under the table?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No. I just want to say that I got a better part.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Congratulations!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Thank you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You seemed to be happy with the new role.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, it's more challenging.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't get stroppy with me it's not my fault!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别_________，那不是我的错！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对我发火</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px 1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px -1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1.4px 0px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1.4px 0px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 3.4px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 0.6px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: square;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读，找不到合适素材的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p border-box;">每日早读一句话之外，想要学习更多语音精讲内容的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">学过语音课程后，想进一步巩固、坚持影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">有一定发音基础，想做影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想要提高英语发音、提高英语听力的你</p><p style="box-sizing: 44%;vertical-align: bottom;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;border-style: solid;border-width: 1px;border-color: rgb(221, 183, 124);align-self: flex-end;padding: 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(236, 215, 182);width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKfsfvibR5NtZ5m1EgagmbQu3ytwZElCTxtSEH8VlQ2AOeQtaWCKT6Po6409lpgx9nDdlWPwv1ic8afw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="110" style="vertical-align: 17);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">扫描二维码快速购买课程</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">或点击推送底部<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">“阅读原文”</span>购买</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px 1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1px -1px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px 1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 0px -1.4px, rgb(18, 17, 17) -1.4px 0px, rgb(18, 17, 17) 1.4px 0px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 3.4px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 0.6px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">什么是影子跟读？</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 1.6;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">1、影子跟读又叫影子练习（shadow-exercise）,也叫跟读训<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">练，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这是一种特别好的练习语音的方法。</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">2、影子跟读，本质是一种“模仿”。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">逐句模仿跟读，“洗掉”固有错音，强化正确发音，不断打磨。</strong>这种方法经济环保，老幼皆宜，方便随时随地练起。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">3、影子跟读首先要学会选材，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">语速适中、难度适中、标准地道的素材</strong>是很重要的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">4、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从“有稿逐句跟读”到“有稿同步跟读”，</strong>用对方法，快速培养“语音感觉”，重塑和强化正确发音。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);font-family: PingFangSC-light;font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持做影子跟读，同步提高语音、听力！</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;font-size: 24px;letter-spacing: 3px;line-height: 1.8;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-shadow: 17) 1.4px 0px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 3px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 1px 1px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 3.4px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 2px 0.6px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 0.6px 2px, rgb(255, 202, 0) 3.4px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">适合人群</em></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: square;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读，找不到合适素材的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family:PingFangSC-light;box-sizing: border-box;">想做影子跟读训练，却不得方法的你</span></p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">每日早读一句话之外，想要学习更多语音精讲内容的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">学过语音课程后，想进一步巩固、坚持影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">有一定发音基础，想做影子跟读的你</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">想要提高英语发音、提高英语听力的你</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">What you do not want </span></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">done</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"> to yourself,</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">do not do to others.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>done /dʌn/ 包含易错音组 /ʌn/。不要发成“当”或“但”。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：want done to/about/with XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">此句中 want done=want to do</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>This is what I <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">want </span></strong></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">done</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想做</strong>的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I would never do something to you that I wouldn't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">want </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">done</span></em></strong> to myself.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我绝不会对你做我不想对自己<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做</strong>的事情。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：do...to XX  对某人做某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't know how he could <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">do</span></em></strong> this <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to</span></em></strong> his own daughter.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我真想象不出他怎么能这样对待自己的女儿。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think he's <span style="text-decoration: underline;">an absolute stinker </span>to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">do</span></em></strong> that <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to</span></em></strong> her.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我认为他那样对她实在是太糟糕了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿拓展：if you want something done well, do it yourself</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em>proverb A phrase warning against delegating tasks to others because they will often do them wrong.</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">Geez, this report is a total mess. I guess it's true what they say—</span><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>if you want something done well, do it yourself</strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">天啊~这份报告简直一团糟。看来他们说的是真的：<strong>想做好，得靠自己。</strong></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> If you want something done well, do it yourself </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Canary </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/kə'neərɪ/ US/kə'nɛri/ (n.)  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">birds yellow finch: a small yellow songbird of the finch family that has been domesticated as a pet and as a show bird. 金丝雀</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：And this is the song of a canary.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这是一只金丝雀在唱歌。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Toxic </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'tɒksɪk/ US/'tɑksɪk/(adj.)  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A toxic substance is poisonous. 有毒的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：I’m addicted to you , Don’t you know that you toxic?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">让我无法自拔，难道你不知道自己是致命的毒药吗(Toxic- Britney Spears)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Screen </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/skriːn/ US/skrin/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">① (vt.)To screen for a disease means to examine people to make sure that they do not have it. (为确定是否患有某病而) 做检查</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The hospital carefully screens volunteers whose job is to provide the newborns human contact while their loved ones are away.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">医院仔细筛选志愿者，这些志愿者的工作是当宝宝的亲人不在旁边时，给予新生儿人体接触。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">② (vt.)To screen people or luggage means to check them using special equipment to make sure they are not carrying a weapon or a bomb. (为确保没有携带武器等而) 检查 (人、行李)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：He says France screens a hundred million air passengers a year at a cost of a billion dollars.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他表示，法国每年对一亿航空乘客进行安检的花费是10亿美元。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">③(vt.) prevent from entering 遮挡、屏蔽、筛选  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Unsuitable candidates were screened out.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那些不合格的候选人被筛选掉了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">④ (vt.)Be screened it is shown in the movie theatre or broadcast on television. 上映 (影片); 播放 (电视节目)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The series is likely to be screened in January.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这部系列剧可能在1月份播放。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Suitability</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/su:tə'biliti/ US/su:tə'biliti/ (n.)  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the quality of having the properties that are right for a specific purpose适合；适当；相配</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：There is no doubt a bout h er suitability for the job.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">毫无疑问，她适合做这个工作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(adj.)suitable  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'suːtəb(ə)l/ US/'sutəbl/  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Someone or something that is suitable for a particular purpose or occasion is right or acceptable for it. 适合的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：I’m not sure it’s suitable for a classroom</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不清楚这个是否适合在教室里使用</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Ad-blocker</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">[ˈæd blɒkə(r)] (n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ad-advertisement </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/əd'vɜːtɪzm(ə)nt/ US/ˌædvɚ'taɪzmənt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Block(vt.)If you block something that is being arranged, you prevent it from being done. 阻止</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pop-up </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">advertisement is a small window containing a menu or advertisement that appears on the screen when you perform particular operations(电脑屏幕上) 弹出的 (菜单、广告) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Pop-up Ad 弹出式广告</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pop-up Store: 快闪店</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Pop Up Play: 画中画</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Deterrent </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/dɪ'ter(ə)nt/US /dɪ'tɝənt/(n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A deterrent is something that prevents people from doing something by making them afraid of what will happen to them if they do it. 威慑物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Nuclear weapons are the ultimate deterrent.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">核武器是终极的威慑力量。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Deter</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/dɪ'tɜː/ US/dɪ'tɝ/(v.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To deter someone from doing something means to make them not want to do it or continue doing it. 阻止</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：I personally hold that blindly worshipping famous people should be deterred from becoming rampant.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我个人认为, 应该阻止盲目崇拜名人成为越来越猖獗的一种现象。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Orthodoxy (-ies)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK /'ɔːθədɒksɪ/ US/'ɔrθədɑksi/ (n.)  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">An orthodoxy is an accepted view about something. 正统观念，正统信仰</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：All the people who aren't satisfied with orthodoxy, who've got independent ideas of their own.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对正统不满，有自己的独立思想。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Orthodox </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'ɔːθədɒks/ US/'ɔrθədɑks/ (adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adhering to what is commonly accepted正统的，传统的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The young generation today don't like orthodox teaching.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当今的年轻一代不喜欢正统的说教。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(adj.)of or relating to the Orthodox Church of the East 东正教会的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Unorthdox(un-)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ʌn'ɔːθədɒks/ US/ʌn'ɔrθə'dɑks/ (adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不寻常的，不正统的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：I realize how it's a bit unorthodox for some people.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道这对一些人来说是很颠覆传统的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: 100%;height: 100%;opacity: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);margin: -0.5em 0px 0px;padding-bottom: 0.5em;border-top-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, border-box;">If the canary became ill or died, they knew (that) th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e a</span></span>ir was toxic. Then we ha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> screen. If you screen something, i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> means you examin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> fo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r i</span></span>t<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">s</span></span> suitability, su<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ch a</span></span>s luggage going th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">rough an</span></span> <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">a</span></span>irport – where they woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>screen fo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r e</span></span>xplosives. Ho<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">w e</span></span>lse ca<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>be use<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span>, Dan?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">如果金丝雀生病或死亡，他们就知道空气中有毒。接下来我们提到了</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">screen</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这个词。检查某物是说检测它的适用性。例如行李经过机场时，要进行审查筛选，看其中是否有爆炸物。这个词还能用于什么地方呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Well, these days you can ge<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t an</span></span> ad-block<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">er on</span></span> your computer tha<span style="text-decoration: border-box;">t</span></span> those annoying po<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">p-u</span></span>p adverts. I ha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">te</span></span> those! After tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> was deterrent. A deterren<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t is a</span></span> thing which stop<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> person from doing something, su<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ch as</span></span> the fear of punishmen<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> fo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r a</span></span> crime. How do you deter your children f<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">rom</span></span> being naughty, Neil?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">如今你可以在电脑上安装一个广告拦截软件，该软件可以筛选出烦人的弹出式广告。我讨厌这种广告！接下来还有威慑一词。威慑物是指阻止某人做某事的东西，例如害怕因犯罪而受到惩罚。孩子们淘气时，你是怎样震慑住他们的？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: That'<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s e</span></span>asy. I jus<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> threaten to remov<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e a</span></span> sticker from their sticker chart.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这很容易。我就威胁他们说撕掉一张贴纸。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Goo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>dea!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好主意！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Finally, we heard orthodoxies. A<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>rthodoxy i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> generall<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y a</span></span>ccepted wa<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y o</span></span>f doing things. It<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>djectiv<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e i</span></span>s orthodox an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> w<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e o</span></span>ften hear its opposi<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">te</span></span> word – unorthodox, meaning unusual. Do you do anything unorthodox, Dan?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">最后我们提到了正统观念。正统观念是指普遍被接受的做事方式。它的形容词形式是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">orthodox</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，我们经常听到它的反义词</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">unorthodox</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，是指不寻常的。你会做一些非正统的事吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Well I love to combine ho<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>sausages an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> col<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> vanilla ice-cream. It's delicious! Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> no one will trus<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> m<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e e</span></span>nough to try!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我喜欢将热香肠和香草冰淇淋一起吃。非常美味。但没有人相信我！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I don'<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> blame them! border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But the Witch looked as if, in a way, she understood the music better than any of them. Her mouth was shut, her lips were pressed together, and her fists were clenched. Ever since the song began she had felt that this whole world was filled with a Magic different from hers and stronger. She hated it. She would have smashed that whole world, or all worlds, to pieces, if it would only stop the singing. The horse stood with its ears well forward, and twitching. Every now and then it snorted and stamped the ground. It no longer looked like a tired old cab-horse; you could now well believe that its father had been in battles.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">女巫看上去似乎比任何人都更能理解那种音乐。她嘴唇紧闭，捏着拳头。歌唱刚开始的时候，她就感到，这个世界笼罩着一种与她的魔力不相同但强大得多的魔力。她恨它。她会把这个世界以至所有的世界都撕成碎片，只要能够阻止那种声音。马站在那里，耳朵前倾并不断地抽动，还时不时用蹄子敲打地面或者打几声响鼻。它看上去不再是一匹劳累不堪的拉车老马，你现在完全可以相信它的父亲当过战马。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我觉得当一名老师非常无聊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 为什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 孩子们总是故意淘气，让你发火。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我不这么想，我觉得他们很可爱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I think teaching is so boring.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Why?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: The children always twist your tail.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I don't think so. I think they are so lovely.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He ___________ the feast and his vomit afterwards.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他对酒席以及后来的呕吐完全没印象了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">had no recollection of</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'>9.17 每日一句：</strong><strong><span style="text-align: justify;">Just be yourself.      </span></strong></p><p style="line-height: 115%;text-align: center;"><strong>做你自己就好。</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="text-align: justify;"></span></strong></p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本周知识点回想</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding: 0px 0px 0px 16px;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-left: 2px dashed rgb(160, 160, 160);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.  你该试着不对别人妄加批评。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.  他在一家超市公然行窃。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.  我近来学得不太好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.  我认为，虚荣心是弗兰克的致命弱点。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.  表面上看，这对夫妇似乎幸福美满。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.  他内心的矛盾和外部世界的争斗有关。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.  你先走，我随后赶上你。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.  你想再喝一杯吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.  她从不甘心于退而求其次。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10. 己所不欲，勿施于人。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: border-box;">没有什么胜利可言，挺住就意味着一切<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>There is no such thing as victory. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Holding on is everything. </p><section><br/></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">背景音乐：</span><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">George Davidson - The Swan</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfb07NCk2toFbuSTb63pGJTnkIFjZvhxo1LR8eFC6fNZ3LLvlWYTHVzdV3fpjs8jpnxbNNggmYI2g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="320" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">作者：里尔克</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">翻译：Gwen</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">朗读：Gwen</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">命运是怎样地，在诗中一去永不复返，</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What is destiny? In poems, it goes without returns. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>它是怎样地，在诗中成为模糊的影象？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How did it gradually turn vague in poems？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有发生过的事物，总是先于我们的判断，</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All that has happened is always preceding our judgements. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我们无从追赶，难以辨认。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is nowhere for us to chase, and no way to tell. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>不要胆怯，如果有死者与你擦肩而过，</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't feel intimidated, if the death passes you by. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>同他们，平静地对视吧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gaze at them with calm.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>无数人的忧伤，使你与众不同。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Countless sorrows distinguish you. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我们目睹了，发生过的事物，</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We witnessed what happened. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>那些时代的豪言壮语，并非为我们所说出。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The heroic words from those times, were not spoken for us.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有何胜利可言？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is no such thing as victory. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">挺住就是一切。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Holding on is everything. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">节选自里尔克的安魂曲之《祭沃尔夫·卡尔克罗伊德伯爵》</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/gDWI0uWrVSHvcvyjNUCSib0YBwdjrtGUuAwgpdte6GO7tYiadhbXiclBxNBW8GJohjw74JosibQx90G6coyJA10xow/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="400" style="vertical-align: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.7515684" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKfb07NCk2toFbuSTb63pGJT5pVhtm7gbNkSmzJ3FiaqWUSm8Nibm6kcWDyQ2OTRlGBxvUdSgNQiaZpaw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="797" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">莱纳·玛利亚·里尔克（1875年12月4日－1926年12月29日）奥地利诗人。诗歌界的风云人物，他的诗曾深受诗歌爱好者的喜爱。早期的创作具有鲜明的布拉格地方色彩和波希米亚民歌风味。是一位重要的德语诗人，除了创作德语诗歌外还撰写小说、剧本以及一些杂文和法语诗歌，其书信集也是里尔克文学作品的一个重要组成部分。对19世纪末的诗歌裁体和风格以及欧洲颓废派文学都有深厚的影响。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 12px;padding-left: 12px;color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen为你</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">读诗</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;float: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">往期精选 </em></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653515328&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=43f2b5dfe7d2c831b164484995d9e2bd&amp;chksm=f7e8ae8dc09f279bb77bdc0eeeb866e064d1b01d90024514cee0b8c285992870e16abaf93dbb&amp;token=1982070592&amp;lang=zh_CN&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect"
