style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本文挖了几个空</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">试着填出来吧～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Looks smaller.看起来很小。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When did he complete it? 他什么时候完成的？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You weren't born yet, and l was 8.你还没出生，我8岁的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Cor busier meets Frank Lloyd Wright.柯布西耶（建筑大师）遇上了法兰克·洛伊·莱特。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, Dad played cards with both of them.你知道吗，爸还跟他们打过牌。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sharing a joint. -Yeah, well....-一起吧。-呃。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can't swim.不会游泳。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There should be a stairway down to the water, a porch, a deck.这里应该弄条楼梯，通到水里，弄一道甲板。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Here, you're in a--ln a box.这里就像在一个盒子里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A glass box with a view to everything that's around you...一个玻璃盒子里，看得到周围的一切，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">... but you can't touch it. 却触摸不到。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No interconnection between you and what you're looking at.在你和你看到的东西之间没有任何联系。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">l don't know, you know. He's got this big maple growing...他还在这里种了这么多枫树。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...right in the middle of the house. -Containment. -在房子的正中央。-是座围墙。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Containment and control.围墙和控制器。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1_________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">l mean, it's beautiful. Seductive, even.我是说，这里很美，很诱人。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But it's incomplete.但却是不完善的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lt was all about him.都是因为他。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2_______________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But you know...但你知道吗，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...l think he wants us to do what he couldn't.我想他希望我们能做到他做不到的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But admitting that...但纵使，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...would mean admitting that he came up short in some way...纵使他只是做了一点点，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...that he could do more.他就会想要做更多。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And that tortures him.那样让他很痛苦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do you remember being here with Mom? 你还记得跟妈妈在这里的时候吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">l remember she tried to make it work here...我记得她想要完成这里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...with us...跟我们一起。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...with him.跟他一起。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Hey, what about Visionary Vanguard? 觉得Visionary Vanguard(梦想先锋兄弟俩策划的公司名) 这名字如何？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What about it? -Come on. -什么东西？-过来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You can't convince me you're gonna be happy building salt boxes for tourists.你可别告诉我，你喜欢去盖那些盐盒式的房子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Nobody's gonna admire you for that.没人会欣赏的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Admire me for that? -Yeah, Visionary Vanguard. -欣赏什么？-梦想家的先锋啊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's your idea.那可是你的想法。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">l can't. But you can keep the name.我不行，不过那名称可以留着。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No, come on. lt's gotta be you and me.别这样，就我和你了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Henry, l'm sorry, l can't.亨利，对不起，我不行。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">l just....我只是……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What? -l've got other plans. -什么？-有别的计划。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You have a girlfriend? 你有女朋友了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-No....不。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No.不是。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What is that? You hesitated. -No, l didn't hesitate. -那是什么？让你这么犹豫-不，我没有犹豫。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Come on, man. l don't have any time for that.嘿，我真的没有时间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What does time have to do with it? 要时间来干什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, you're gonna think l'm crazy.你可能会以为我疯了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="height: 100%;width: 100%;line-height:
